British Foreign Secretary Demands Results; Albania Willing to Negotiate Directly with Italy

But the Peace Talks Must Be Watched by Neutral Observers; If Italy Accepts, It Will Begin Within the Next Week

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen decided yesterday to re-entrust Chairman Madariaga and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol to explore the opinions of Italy and Albania regarding the peace issue. The Albanian representative, the country's ambassador to France, Gjevaheri, has accepted the request of British Foreign Secretary Eden, stating that he is willing to conduct direct negotiations with Italy, but requests that neutral observers closely monitor the talks. These observers may be concurrently held by Madariaga, but this is uncertain. If Italy can accept this procedure, then negotiations between Italy and Albania can begin within the next week. It is not yet known whether Italy will immediately cease fire or wait until Italy and Albania reach an agreement before ceasing fire. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

(Geneva) Regarding the dispute between Italy and Albania, the Albanian representative, the country's ambassador to France, Gjevaheri, visited British Foreign Secretary Eden and stated to him that his government is now prepared to conduct peace talks, but the negotiations should be conducted within the scope of the League of Nations. Eden then consulted with Madariaga, chairman of the League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen, and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. Observers believe that Britain and several other national delegations firmly believe that concrete steps must be taken to resolve the dispute between Italy and Albania before they can leave Geneva. Therefore, the Committee of Thirteen may have to extend its session until after Easter. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

(Rome) The League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen entrusted Chairman Madariaga and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol yesterday to inquire with the two parties involved whether they could cease hostilities before April 14. Observers here claim that it is difficult for Italy to comply. Its reply will probably not be more than two points: 1. After the Committee of Thirteen proposed peace negotiations in March of this year, Albanian troops first attacked Italian troops. 2. Wherever the Italian army goes, the natives applaud and celebrate as liberators and are now assisting the Italian army in pursuing the troops belonging to the Albanian Emperor. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

Britain and France Have Different Priorities on the Italian Issue

The Committee of Thirteen Discussed for a Long Time

(Geneva) The Committee of Thirteen met today for a long time to consider whether to immediately begin peace talks between Italy and Albania. After discussion, it was resolved to authorize Chairman Madariaga and League Secretary-General Avenol to visit the Italian representative to the League Council, Aloisi, to inquire about Italy's attitude towards a ceasefire. According to British Foreign Secretary Eden, if the efforts of the two cannot agree on a ceasefire, the British government must reserve its attitude. Eden also firmly stated that there should be no further delay. We must make the war end immediately and negotiate within the League of Nations framework. French Foreign Minister Flandin did not think it was appropriate to act hastily and proposed that the two be given until April 14 to receive a reply from Rome. Eden replied resentfully that the Committee did not seem to be accused of acting hastily. The Committee should have discussed the use of poison gas by Italian troops in Albania and resolved to establish a small committee of public law experts to review the violation of the 1925 convention prohibiting the use of gas. The Committee also discussed whether to discuss it or whether it should be handed over to the League of Nations Council for discussion. The British delegation sent a document to the Committee based on reports from Abyssinians and non-Abyssinians, stating the use of poison gas by Italian troops and presenting the evidence of Dr. Mele, a British Red Cross volunteer, Dr. Mark, a worker in the British ambulance team, Dr. White Roswell of Ireland, and a talk from Dr. Junod, an official of the International Red Cross, indicating that they had treated many Abyssinian soldiers poisoned by gas in Abyssinia. The Committee then adjourned until 4 p.m. (Reuters dispatch from the 9th)

(Geneva) A special dispatch from our agency's diplomatic correspondent reveals that after the League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen met today, it has been proven that Britain and France have different opinions on resolving the dispute between Italy and Albania. France advocates that if the war between Italy and Albania is to be stopped quickly, sanctions must also be stopped at the same time. This is the same as Foreign Minister Flandin's speech in the House of Representatives on March 20 (in which he said that both the war between Italy and Albania and sanctions against Italy should be stopped quickly). In Britain, it is advocated that if Italy refuses to negotiate, sanctions should be intensified because of the country's use of suffocating gas. Foreign Secretary Eden also said, "The fate of Europe depends on whether this issue can be resolved. Assuming that London, Paris, and Berlin are attacked by toxic gas, what will be the damage? We cannot help but be frightened when we think about this." Regarding this matter, Foreign Minister Flandin believed that the Italian and Albanian armies were reported to have committed atrocities, and if the Red Cross needs to conduct an investigation, it should be done without distinction. However, this kind of problem is related to combat methods, and the Committee of Thirteen has no right to make a decision. Therefore, it proposed to organize a committee of legal experts to investigate whether there was any violation of wartime laws. The British delegation recently issued a document stating the various evidence of the Italian army's use of suffocating gas, including the reports submitted by the doctors of the British Red Cross ambulance team and the notes repeatedly sent by the Albanian government to the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch from the 8th)

League of Nations Investigates Italian Use of Poison Gas; British Representative Presents Various Pieces of Evidence; A Legal Staff Committee is Now Organized to Handle It

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen appointed a legal expert staff committee yesterday to draft a report on the combat methods of the Italian and Albanian armies, so that it can be submitted for discussion today. It is known that the Committee of Thirteen has decided to discuss it at 4 p.m. today. According to general knowledge, the results of the study by the expert staff committee are that the protests submitted by the two parties involved, Italy and Albania, regarding the combat methods of the other party must first be discussed by the League of Nations Council, because this issue is not within the scope of the Committee's authority. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

(Geneva) The Committee of Thirteen continued its meeting at 4 p.m. this afternoon. British Foreign Secretary Eden presented a brief memorandum on the spot for discussion. The memorandum was related to the issue of the Italian army's use of poison gas. After a long debate, the Committee passed a resolution to establish another expert committee to study the legal point of view of this violation of the international convention on wartime affairs, whether the Committee of Thirteen has the right to jurisdiction, or should be handed over to the League of Nations Council for resolution. Regarding the mediation of the dispute between Italy and Albania, it was also resolved to ask the Chairman to quickly conduct preliminary talks with the Italian representative to the League Council, Aloisi, who is currently in Geneva, together with League Secretary-General Avenol. Once there is a clue, formal discussions will be held. At this point, the meeting adjourned until tomorrow afternoon. (National News dispatch from the 8th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council's Committee of Thirteen met this afternoon at 4 p.m. and ended at 6:30 p.m. The legal experts of the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Badevant, the legal experts of the British Foreign Office, Malkin, and the Spanish representative Ariwen were appointed to form a legal expert staff committee to specialize in studying the combat methods of the Italian and Albanian armies, especially the issue of the Italian army's violation of the 1925 Geneva Protocol and the use of suffocating gas in Albania (according to this protocol, it was signed on September 20, 1925, stating that the signatory countries prohibit the use of various toxic gases and microbial methods in combat). The Committee must submit a report when the Committee of Thirteen continues its meeting at 4 p.m. tomorrow afternoon. In addition, the Committee of Thirteen also re-entrusted Chairman Madariaga and League Secretary-General Avenol to explore the opinions of the two parties involved, Italy and Albania, regarding the peace issue. The Italian representative Aloisi will come here tomorrow, and Madariaga will meet with him at that time. (Havas dispatch from the 8th)

U.S. Investment in China: Armed Protection Ultimately Does More Harm Than Good - Words from the Secretary-General of the Anti-War Association

Kansai: Mr. Libby, Secretary-General of the American Anti-War Association, declared today that no matter how much money is spent on armaments, it will be difficult to protect American investments in China. He predicts that the U.S. military budget for the coming year will exceed $1,000,000,000. He also stated that American investments in China amount to only $130,000,000, but if one were to resort to war to protect this amount of investment, it would cost a huge sum of $40,000,000,000. Spain - Cabinet Resigns, Asked to Stay

Elect New President Within Five Weeks

Madrid: After the resignation of former President Zamorra, Prime Minister Azana submitted his resignation to interim President Baliwo, but Baliwo asked him to stay, so he withdrew his resignation. According to well-informed sources, former President Zamorra originally intended to appeal to the Constitutional Court regarding the results of the House of Representatives vote, but has now abandoned this plan and will soon move his family to the city of Puerto Rico in the state of Cordova to live as a commoner. At this time, who is the most promising successor to the presidency? Speculation abounds in various quarters. Generally, the most respected candidate is Baliwo himself. However, Baliwo's political friends said that he is currently the Speaker of the House of Representatives and the leader of the United Republican Party, and his political status is extremely high. Moreover, as for the position of Prime Minister, apart from the current Prime Minister Azana, Baliwo is the most qualified. Therefore, he may not be willing to accept the election as head of state. Political figures believe that Roman, the head of the Republican National Party, may have hopes of succeeding as president. Although he has not actively participated in political activities, the left-wing People's Front, which impeached Zamorra, fully supports him. (Eighth Havas News Agency Telegram)

Madrid: Since President Zamora formally announced his resignation, according to the provisions of the current Spanish constitution, the election of the new president should be handled within five weeks from the date of the president's formal resignation. In other words, a qualified presidential elector must be elected before May 14 of this year to help the Congress elect a new president. According to general observations, the three candidates with the highest voices for the new president are: Mr. Baliwo, former Prime Minister and current Speaker of the Senate, Mr. Arponas, former President of the Constitutional Draft Review Court, Mr. Pesters, former Speaker of the Senate and leader of the moderate faction of the Socialist Party. U.S. Presidential Election

Roosevelt and Borah Compete

Milwaukee: The progressives of Wisconsin mostly support Roosevelt as a presidential candidate, but the Republicans in this state mostly support Borah. Judging from the results that have been announced in 2,190 of the 2,919 electoral districts, Roosevelt received a total of 292,530 votes, and Borah received 129,584 votes. The Progressives and La Follette's Third Party are now in cahoots with the Democratic Party. However, Borah has already obtained a majority of the 24 delegates designated to attend the Republican National Convention. Therefore, in the presidential election between Roosevelt and Borah, it is still impossible to predict who will win. (Eighth National Telegram)

France's Second Memorandum

(Paris) In addition to submitting the first memorandum in response to the German memorandum, France also submitted a second memorandum detailing the peace plan, which begins by saying, "The Government of the French Republic, in making this proposal, aims to maintain the honor of all nations and have them fulfill their promises, respect the equal rights of all nations, encourage international trade, and achieve universal, complete, and lasting peace, and by genuinely limiting armaments, to take steps to reduce armaments, in order to achieve genuine peace."

This plan is based on the following principles:

Equality of rights and respect for international obligations must be ensured. The French government believes that if peace depends on the needs and desires of various nations, then peace will ultimately be unattainable.

The rule of international law should have mandatory and substantial guarantees.

Hegemony is not allowed. The French government believes that all countries should be able to freely relinquish part of their sovereignty under certain circumstances, especially in the matter of armaments. If there are disparities in the military strength of various countries, a universal mutual assistance pact can be concluded to remedy this.

As for politically viable measures, the French government believes that the European continent is the standard region for organizing a collective security system. However, if the whole of Europe is considered too vast to become a single entity based on the principle of mutual assistance, it can be divided into several regions, thereby establishing several regional public bodies. Within the framework of the League of Nations, a pan-European committee can be organized to take on organizational matters, which is also possible. Changes to the existing borders of various countries must be implemented only with the mutual agreement of the countries concerned. However, countries may not demand changes to the existing borders within 25 years. In addition, the countries concerned must agree on appropriate measures for the fulfillment of treaty obligations, especially with regard to arms reduction, which should include military means. Regarding this matter, each signatory to the general European convention or regional conventions shall designate army, air force, and naval units to be placed under the command of the League of Nations and the pan-European committee. This committee shall also monitor the fulfillment of the obligations of various provisions. Once the mutual assistance system is organized, genuine arms reduction can be realized. When the pan-European committee discusses the issue of arms reduction, it only needs a two-thirds majority to make a decision. All current and future treaties in Europe must be submitted to the committee for record, and those that conflict with the general European convention or regional conventions may be declared invalid by the committee.

The memorandum then puts forward five economic proposals, believing that economic improvement is primarily to maintain peace. After the establishment of a European political organization, economic organization must be started. The key points are as follows:

European countries should adopt a preferential tariff system and mutually conclude tariff treaties to develop trade.

Sign international agreements or European agreements to limit current tariff protection policies, implement a tariff truce, and establish an international trade court to prevent the arbitrary abolition of commercial agreements.

Organize a monetary credit system within Europe.

The distribution of colonial resources should be corrected so that European countries can obtain the necessary raw materials.

The above-mentioned measures should be handled by a special committee established by the pan-European committee and submitted to an international conference for discussion. All member states or non-member states of the League of Nations should be invited to participate in this conference.

The second memorandum then concludes that this peace plan is not in conflict with the League of Nations covenant, but is integrated with it. The principles contained in the League of Nations are the highest laws on which this plan is based. (Eighth Havas News Agency Telegram)

British Blue Book - Publishes Documents on Germany

Total of 59 Types

(London) The Cabinet released a Blue Book this morning containing 59 documents, of which a long telegram from Foreign Secretary Eden to Ambassador to Germany Sir Phipps on March 26 of this year is the most important. The telegram details the diplomatic talks conducted by the British government from June 1924 to March 7 of this year (the date Germany abolished the Locarno Treaty) to organize a European peace mechanism. This talk can be divided into five parts: Negotiations for the conclusion of the Eastern European Convention, from June 1934 to May 1935 (the time of the signing of the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty); The exchange of documents between the countries concerned regarding the question of whether the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty is in conflict with the Locarno Treaty, from May 1935 to August of the same year; Progress on negotiations regarding the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Convention during the same period; Negotiations regarding the Sky Convention and the limitation of air force armaments; Attempts made to continue negotiations with Germany from November 1935 to March of this year. The telegram briefly states that "In the view of the British government, the original French draft of the Eastern European Convention had shortcomings in that the guarantees it gave to France and the Soviet Union were not equal to the guarantees it gave to Germany. For this reason, Britain and France held talks in London on July 11, 1934, to remedy this. As a result, the following approach was drafted: that the Netherlands, the Soviet Union, Germany, Czechoslovakia, Finland, and the Baltic countries (Lithuania, Latvia, and Estonia) conclude a mutual guarantee of non-aggression and mutual consultation convention, and that the Soviet Union accept the obligations of the guarantor states of the Locarno Treaty for France and Germany, while France accept the obligations stipulated in the above-mentioned mutual non-aggression and mutual consultation convention for Germany and Russia, provided that its obligations are not in conflict with the obligations France bears under the League of Nations Covenant." After this approach was determined, Britain immediately urged the countries concerned, especially Germany and Poland, to accept it, but neither country agreed. Germany also made it clear in the autumn of 1934 that it was willing to maintain peace in Eastern Europe in a way that was acceptable to both sides. Therefore, France and the Soviet Union signed a protocol in Geneva on December 5 of that year, mutually agreeing that neither country would participate in any negotiations that aimed at concluding bilateral or multilateral agreements that would hinder the establishment of the Eastern European Convention. On March 25, 1935, former British Foreign Secretary Simon and Foreign Secretary Eden (then Lord Privy Seal) went to Berlin together. German leader Hitler informed the British cabinet members of the outline of the proposed Eastern European Convention, the content of which advocated that Eastern European countries conclude bilateral non-aggression pacts and separately conclude arbitration, conciliation, and consultation agreements, and that each of these countries provide a promise not to assist aggressor countries to supplement this. "At the time, leader Hitler also stated that if the above-mentioned bilateral agreements were to be included in a multilateral agreement system, the German government would not oppose it. However, since Germany did not approve of mutual assistance methods, it would not be convenient to join the mutual assistance convention. During the meeting between Britain, France, and Italy in Stressa last April, the German government, at the request of British Ambassador Sir Phipps, issued an announcement stating that Germany was prepared to participate in the Eastern European Convention in accordance with the outline outlined on March 25, provided that the other signatory countries agreed on mutual assistance methods, but with the condition that the mutual assistance methods be included in individual agreements. After this announcement was issued, the French government decided not to wait any longer and immediately negotiated a mutual assistance convention with the Soviet Union." At that time, Britain asked France whether the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty was in conflict with the Locarno Treaty. France immediately replied that "France has put forward an absolute condition for the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty, that is, the obligations of this treaty are not only subject to the restrictions of the application of the League of Nations Covenant, but also subject to the restrictions of the application of the Locarno Treaty. The Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty was finally signed and established on May 2 of last year. On the 21st of the same month, German leader Hitler delivered a speech stating that France and the Soviet Union had already formed a military alliance. What kind of impact and consequences this agreement will have on the treaty obligations borne by the countries concerned by the Locarno Treaty, Germany hopes to obtain an accurate explanation. As far as Germany is concerned, the German government will fulfill all obligations arising from the Locarno Treaty." Afterwards, the countries concerned exchanged documents on the issue of whether the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty was in conflict with the Locarno Treaty. Former British Foreign Secretary Sir Hoare ordered Ambassador to Germany Sir Phipps on July 5 of last year to express to the German government that the rights and obligations of all signatories to the Locarno Treaty, including Germany, have not been harmed or changed by the establishment of the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty. It is hoped that the German government will recognize this. In the same month, the British government again contacted Germany, wanting to repeat the judgment on the Eastern European Convention. Regarding this matter, German Deputy Foreign Minister Bulow informed the British representative on August 22 of last year that the German government could not make any statement before October. (Eighth Havas News Agency Telegram)

Italy First to Implement Air Force Conscription System Among All Countries in the World

(Rome) Prime Minister Mussolini hurriedly convened a cabinet meeting today and passed an order approving the selection of a portion of each year's conscripts to join the air force. As a result, Italy has become the first country in the world to implement an air force conscription system. (Eighth Reuters Telegram)

Hopeh Provincial Reconstruction Department Expedites Spring Work on Various Rivers

(Tianjin) In order to expedite spring work on various rivers, the Hopeh Provincial Reconstruction Department has dispatched supervisors to organize temporary engineering offices together with the directors of various river affairs bureaus, purchase materials, and start work immediately, with a deadline for completion before the flood season. The spring work budget is estimated at 64,000 yuan for the Yongding River, of which a portion has been allocated by the Economic Commission; over 90,000 yuan for the Yellow River; and a total of 58,000 yuan for the North-South Canal, Ziya River, and Daqing River, all of which are allocated by the provincial government. (Ninth Central News Agency Telegram)

(Tianjin) To prevent flooding this year, the Hopeh Reconstruction Department established the Winter River Engineering Office early and started spring flood control works. The Yongding River flood control fee is 64,000 yuan, allocated by the Economic Commission; the Ziya River, North-South Canal, and Daqing River project funds are 58,000 yuan, allocated by the Reconstruction Department; and the Yellow River flood risk fee is 90,000 yuan, allocated by the province. The Reconstruction Department has also assigned river supervisors to depart for various rivers to supervise the work. A breach occurred in the Ziya River in Jinghai County, obstructing water flow and causing a collapse. More than 30,000 mu of spring wheat along the river were flooded. County Magistrate Guan Guangyu went to the breach site on the 9th to supervise workers to rush to close the breach. (Ninth Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Municipal Government, because the Tianjin Yuyuan, Baocheng, and Beiyang three major yarn factories, which are famous in Beiyang industry, are all being negotiated and sold to Japanese, feels that this is a very serious matter for the national industry. Today, the Social Affairs Bureau summoned representatives of various factories to study relief methods to avoid being controlled by foreigners. It also ordered detailed planning for fundamental strategies to relieve industry and commerce. (Ninth Telegram)

Ministry of Justice Clarifies Ambiguities Regarding Gambling Crimes

(Nanjing) The Zhejiang Higher Court submitted a request for clarification regarding ambiguities in gambling crimes. The Ministry of Justice explained: 1. Gambling for property within one's own residence or household, not in a public place or a place accessible to the public, does not constitute a crime under Article 266 of the Criminal Law. 2. If the homeowner or head of household, with the intent to profit, provides their residence for gambling and skims from the winnings, they shall be jointly held criminally liable. However, those who are injured or those who gamble are not committing a crime since it's neither a public or publicly accessible place. 3. If there is credible evidence that gambling crimes are being committed in the residence of a current official and the situation is urgent, judicial police may directly search the premises in accordance with Article 131, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Procedure Law. However, the points raised in the document do not involve any circumstances under Articles 267 or 268 of the Criminal Law, and since no crime has been committed, arrests may not be carried out. (9th Special Dispatch)

Han Dynasty Stone Carvings Discovered in Xuzhou

(Xuzhou) Two large Han dynasty stone carvings were discovered in Xubu. They are carved with depictions of Confucius Traveling Around the States. Antique dealers sold them to the Japanese, but the political and police authorities seized them. Local gentry have come forward to negotiate, and the owner of the stones, a Mr. Gao, has donated them to the library for display. The matter was resolved on the 9th. On the 10th, they will be transported from the station to the library for public viewing. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Regarding the change in affiliation of the North China Water Conservancy Association to the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, a person in charge of the National Economic Commission told reporters on the 9th that the Central Government had previously resolved to unify the national water administration, with the Commission serving as the national headquarters for water conservancy. The North China Water Conservancy Association is also subordinate to the Commission, and its annual operating expenses are also allocated by the Commission. Regulations for Rewarding Antiquities Announced

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan announced the Regulations for Rewarding Antiquities on the 9th and issued a circular for its implementation. The key points are: Those eligible to apply for rewards include those who report discoveries, donors, and those who deposit antiquities with public institutions for academic research and display. Rewards are divided into cash prizes and certificates of merit. The cash prize is limited to 10,000 yuan. Applicants shall submit an application to the Ministry of Interior or the competent authority, which will be forwarded to the Central Antiquities Committee for verification. Japanese Military Representative Stationed in Tianjin, Matsumuro Takayoshi, Arrives in Beiping

Japanese Military Ordered to Advance to the Great Wall Line to Preside Over Hebei-Chahar Diplomatic Negotiations

Beiping Correspondence: Regarding the Hebei-Chahar situation, after Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, went to Tianjin last month to exchange views with relevant parties in a private capacity, it is now known that the discussions have largely taken shape as of the 30th of last month. In the near future, both parties can begin negotiations based on the agreed scope.

Regarding Hebei-Chahar diplomacy, before Doihara returned to his country, the Japanese Kwantung Army came forward, and Doihara's qualification was as a special representative of the Japanese Kwantung Army. After Doihara's return, Matsumuro Takayoshi succeeded him, but his qualification was changed to a representative of the Japanese army in Tianjin, responsible for all future Japanese negotiations in North China.

Matsumuro once served as an advisor to Feng Yuxiang during the National Army era and was very congenial with Song Zheyuan and Xiao Zhenying. His appointment to this position leads to general speculation that future negotiations may be better than in the past. Matsumuro arrived in Beiping from Tianjin on the morning of the 6th to set up the Beiping Representative Office of the Japanese Garrison in Tianjin. He began working within days. The organization is divided into four sections, with Hamada as his assistant. On the 6th and 7th, Matsumuro met with reporters from China, Britain, the United States, Germany, and France at the Fusang Hotel. The content of his talks varied due to his position. In general, he spoke relatively politely to the Chinese press, adopted a tone resembling a statement to the Japanese press, and used the full range of diplomatic rhetoric to the British, American, German, and French reporters, without committing to anything.

In summary, Matsumuro has prepared to begin Hebei-Chahar diplomatic negotiations. Song Zheyuan is also scheduled to return to Beiping within a week to take charge personally. According to unofficial news, the Japanese Central Military Department seemed to have issued a certain order on the 2nd of this month, dispatching the [unclear] division to advance to the Great Wall line. At the same time, the counties in the "war zone" have been busy vacating houses in recent days. However, the relevant parties here say they have not received such reports. The truth will soon be confirmed.

Matsumuro Expresses Views on Sino-Japanese Diplomacy

The Hebei-Chahar diplomatic issue was once stalled after the Japanese representative Doihara returned to his country. Matsumuro Takayoshi, attached to the command of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin, arrived in Beiping on the 6th at 11:38 AM on the 6th train of the Beining Railway. After getting off the train, he went to the Fusang Hotel to rest. He is scheduled to establish an office attached to the command of the Japanese garrison in Dongjiaominxiang around the 10th. Beiping Mayor Qin Dechun hosted a banquet on the 7th to welcome Matsumuro. When reporters interviewed Matsumuro at the Fusang Hotel, Matsumuro was wearing a Japanese major general-level military uniform and spoke Chinese fluently. However, he said with a smile that he had been away from China for a long time and had forgotten most of his Chinese. He then switched to speaking Japanese, which was translated by an interpreter. His remarks were recorded as follows: "In the future, all negotiations in North China will be handled by the representative of the Japanese government attached to the command of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin. I came to Beiping as a representative of the garrison command and will be stationed in Beiping permanently, responsible for all communication and liaison matters between China and Japan. I will not leave Beiping in the short term and have not prepared to visit Jin, Chahar, or Suiyuan. I will set up an office attached to the command in Beiping, but I definitely do not intend to set up a special agency. The office organization is simple, with only one assistant besides myself. The office is currently being set up and will take about ten days to establish. Regarding the North China issue, because I have been away from China for a long time, I am not clear about the situation. I only saw that the lives of the people seemed more difficult than when I last came to China on the way to Beiping. Regarding Hebei-Chahar negotiations, because I have just arrived in China from Japan, my mind is like a blank sheet of paper and I have no impressions. Therefore, I have no comments to make. However, to seek Sino-Japanese friendship, both parties should be based on sincerity, otherwise it will be difficult to achieve the goal. I met Chairman Song Zheyuan several times in Tianjin. Because I am an old friend of Song, we were happy to meet after a long separation. Besides reminiscing about the past, we did not discuss anything else. I am not very familiar with the increase in troops by the Japanese garrison in North China. Regarding the communist bandits disturbing Shanxi, I believe that the spread of the communist scourge is not just a problem for China, but a major problem for the entire East Asia. China is suffering from the communist scourge, and Japan is also deeply concerned. Therefore, Japan attaches great importance to this. As for the current situation of the anti-communist military in Shanxi Province, because it is an internal problem of China, I do not want to express any opinion." In addition to making remarks to the press, Matsumuro also issued his inaugural address as follows: "I am very happy to be newly appointed in the old capital, which was once the crown of cultural regions in the world, and to work with old friends towards new tasks. My task is to work with the officials and people of North China, based on established policies, to quickly complete the clarification of North China to establish a foundation for East Asian peace. However, the communist scourge has spread to Shanxi Province, which is known as a peaceful homeland. Wherever they pass, even chickens and dogs are silent, and the area becomes desolate. Moreover, there are actions in various places that are ignorant of the overall situation in East Asia. Therefore, it can be said that the current situation in North China has reached the greatest crisis and is in a state of suffering. Therefore, I believe that now is the time to rise up and sweep away the 'bad elements' and raise the clear banner of 'anti-communism.' In particular, the reddening of North China is something that the Japanese garrison, which is in an important position to protect Japanese residents, cannot ignore. We also sincerely hope to clarify North China as soon as possible, so that it can become a 'land of happiness' for the people. The entire Japanese nation is determined to make any sacrifices for this. Although I am of limited ability, since I have been ordered to take this position, what I hope from the wise officials and people is that they will realize that violating the policy of 'Sino-Japanese cooperation' is an act of 'destroying the country and misleading the people,' and fully observe and understand the current situation and the true intentions of the Japanese side, and discuss the true path of Sino-Japanese cooperation and saving the country and ensuring the well-being of the people, and resolutely work together to thoroughly prevent communism and make North China clear." (7th)

Japanese Textile Industry Extends Influence Towards Tianjin

Cheaply Taking Over Bankrupt Yarn Factories, Toyo Textile Company Building New Factory

Tianjin Correspondence: The Japanese textile industry, under the guidance of the South Manchuria Railway Company, has recently decided to invest in North China. It has been decided to build large-scale yarn factories in Tianjin, including the Toyo Textile Company, the Dai Nippon Textile Company, and the Kanebo Textile Company. The latter two are progressing more slowly in their investigations, so they are currently only buying closed yarn factories in Tianjin, intending to改造 machines to engage in both spinning and weaving. Kanebo Textile Company plans to also set up a woolen factory in addition to these two businesses, intending to purchase raw materials in Jingjiakou to spin wool, wool fabrics, and other goods in Tianjin. In Tianjin, the Baocheng and Beiyang factories, known as the six major yarn factories in Beiyang, are both heavily indebted. The board of directors has cleared them multiple times, but without success. Taking advantage of the factories' plight, Kanebo Textile Company, due to various relationships, is unwilling to come forward itself, so it has entrusted the Tianjin Yuda Yarn Factory to contact Baocheng on its behalf, and the Yicheng Foreign Firm, a shareholder of Yuda, is acting as the nominal investor, funding a lease or a one-time payment for takeover. The two sides are in the process of negotiating the terms. The shareholders of Baocheng are hesitant to sell, so they are willing to sign a contract to lease the factory to Yicheng for a short period of time, but they are still hesitant to sell it outright. The Dai Nippon Textile Company is in contact with the Beiyang Yarn Factory, while the Toyo Textile Company also wants to buy the Beiyang Yarn Factory. The owner of the Beiyang Yarn Factory, Zhang Ruiting, is willing to sell to the Toyo Textile Company because it offered a higher price. The Dai Nippon Textile Company is still working hard to win it over due to business competition. In addition, after the Yuyuan Spinning Mill stopped production and cleared its assets for more than a year, it originally planned to be reorganized as the Xinyi Company, recruiting new shares to maintain operations. However, because of losses of more than five million yuan over the years, Chairman Lu Chongzhi went to Shanghai to contact banks, financial institutions, and industrialists for loans, but waited in Shanghai for several months without results. The factory owes the Japanese Okura Trading Company more than three million yuan, and more than three million yuan of stock has fallen into Japanese hands, secretly controlled by the Japanese. It has no ability to recover, and the Japanese creditors are pressing for payment, so there are discussions of selling. The Kanebo Textile Company is in the process of buying it, and the terms have been agreed upon. The approximate price is 3.3 million yuan, which, after offsetting debts, leaves nothing. The Kanebo Textile Company is preparing to complete the takeover of the factory this month and start production next month. Yuyuan is the largest of the six yarn factories in Beiyang, with a capital of five million yuan and 30 years of operation. The main factory is divided into four branch factories: Yuan, Heng, Li, and Zhen, with 70,000 spindles. Although the machines are old, they are sturdy and durable. If managed properly, it can still be successful. Now it has been bought by the Japanese, which is a great loss to the industrial circles of North China.

The Toyo Textile Company is not only buying existing yarn factories in Tianjin, but also plans to build a large yarn factory with 150,000 spindles in Tianjin. It has acquired two plots of vacant land in the Fourth Special District of Tianjin (former Belgian Concession), each about a hundred acres, located in front of the Fourth Special District Public Office, to the left and right of the Texaco Petroleum Storage. The company acquired them at a low price and has completed all the formalities. Construction is scheduled to begin on April 15th and be completed by the end of this year. The first installation will be of 50,000 spindles, and 5,000 hardworking and enduring male and female workers will be recruited from Dalian to engage in spinning. At the same time, the company will continue to buy land and continue to build, aiming to reach the capacity to accommodate 150,000 spindles. According to the observation of the Japanese textile industry, the yarn sales in North China are very good, and the cotton production is also rich. If managed legally, Japanese merchants can monopolize the sales markets in the five provinces.

The Cultural Enterprise Department of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in order to help the Japanese yarn industry extend its influence in North China, is cooperating with the South Manchuria Railway Company to invest in eastern Hebei and Jiaodong, providing farmers with cash and lending 100,000 catties of cotton seeds from the Korean Governor-General's Office to supply agricultural use and experiment with improved cotton planting, so as to facilitate the supply of raw materials. Recently, the puppet Hebei (East) government is also renting a thousand acres of land in Tongxian to experiment with planting cotton, probably also to supply raw materials. (6th)

Bubbling Poisonous Atmosphere in Bengbu

Three Thousand Smokers Consume Two Thousand Yuan Daily; A Detoxification Center Established to Thoroughly Eradicate the Problem

Bengbu Correspondence: In recent years, white powder has become exceptionally prevalent in Bengbu. Unscrupulous merchants and local ruffians secretly transport and sell it for people to smoke, profiting from it. This type of drug, originally called heroin, is known as "Lao Hai" among Anhui people. It is purely extracted from the essence of opium, and its harm is extremely severe. It can not only lead to national ruin but also to the extinction of the race. Bengbu is a den of iniquity in northern Anhui, and the number of degenerate individuals addicted to this bad habit is increasing daily. Furthermore, some members of the underworld, tired of the old, are turning to white powder. Initially, smokers believe it is cheaper and more convenient than opium, but after prolonged addiction, the opposite is true. Those deeply addicted develop an earthy complexion and, at most, die from the drug within four or five years. It is impossible to avoid the destruction of life and the weakening of the race, harming the country and the people. There is truly nothing more egregious than this. According to those concerned about the poisonous atmosphere, it is estimated that no fewer than three thousand people in Bengbu consume this type of drug, spending approximately two thousand yuan daily, amounting to over seven hundred thousand yuan annually. The wealthy drug dealers have been known as the "Four Great Kongs," and there are numerous individuals secretly engaged in retail sales. Although military and police agencies occasionally make arrests, the traffickers, unafraid of the law, continue to take risks and transport drugs as before. To thoroughly eradicate drugs, the Public Security Bureau has established a detoxification center, sending arrested addicts for compulsory detoxification. After their addiction is broken, they are released only after providing a written guarantee promising to accept the death penalty if they relapse. If sellers are apprehended, they are sent to the Fengyang County Government to be severely punished according to the drug prohibition regulations. Although the authorities strictly prohibit drugs, the number of smokers and sellers has not decreased, which is a great concern for the future of our people. (April 8)

Two Hunan and Hubei Supervisory Envoys Secretly Investigate Wuhan Dike Defenses

Letters Sent to Responsible Agencies Urging Attention

Hankou Correspondence: As the spring flood season approaches, the water level in the Yangtze and Han Rivers is rising daily. According to the Jianghan Customs water level mark, it rose another 1.2 meters yesterday, the 7th, totaling 4.2 meters in the past week, equivalent to over ten English feet. All provincial and local dikes are being hastily reinforced by the responsible agencies. The Two Hunan and Hubei Supervisory Envoy's Office, mindful of the devastation caused by last year's floods, recognizes that this year's major flood season is rapidly approaching. Many dikes and embankments have not been repaired or are unlikely to be completed on time. In addition to dispatching personnel to various locations for investigation, the office has specially assigned counselors to secretly investigate the condition of dikes and embankments in Wuhan. The current investigation reveals the situation of important dikes and embankments in Wuchang, Hanyang, and Hankou. Letters have been sent to the responsible agencies urging them to expedite construction. In Wuchang, the body of the Wuhui Dike is mostly composed of sand. Areas where the Shi Dike's slope is damaged should be repaired as soon as possible to prevent wave erosion. Particular attention should be paid to the Tangfang section of the dike, where the dike foot is hollow. It is hoped that the responsible parties will gather funds and begin construction as soon as possible. An inquiry has been sent to the Wuchang County Government, requesting their attention. In Hankou, the Changfeng North and South Embankments have 22 major and minor breaches in the South Embankment, and dike funds have not yet been secured. The North Embankment has 21 major and minor breaches and is still being piled. These two embankments are crucial to the safety of Hankou and urgently need repair. Letters have been sent to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau and the Hankou Municipal Government for inquiry. In Hanyang, the breaches in the Yongfeng Embankment should be repaired as soon as possible. The Provincial Government has been requested to expedite construction. (April 7)

The Social Foundations of Fascism (Part Two)

— By Joseph Barncs, Translated by Bu Ren

Naturally, they view fascism as a genuine social revolution, as a doctrine that shifts power from one class to another or to the state. They anticipate that the middle class, in the initial compromise with big capital, will have sufficient strength and vitality. They fantasize that, at some point, the development of national ideals will lead to the nationalization of all these enterprises. Many of fascism's slightly mystical aspects, and its emphasis on the efficiency of war, are clearly intended to create a mass conception of loyalty to the nation. The ultimate concrete plans of the ruling nation, whether in Italy or Germany, are not yet clear. Fascism and National Socialism's disdain for plans and the frank opportunism of theory are inevitably subject to such criticism.

From the socialist perspective, all of this is pure posturing. Strachey, in his "The Nature of Capitalist Crisis," states: "Fascists consider themselves an independent class force based on the petty bourgeoisie. This entire concept is completely fictitious. In reality, fascism is always and everywhere a tool, not belonging to the petty bourgeoisie, which uses big capitalists as its unwitting allies, but to the big capitalists, who use the petty bourgeoisie as fools."

Socialists point out that fascism has never "held" power in any country; its power was given by capitalist powers when they needed to recruit agitators and private armies to maintain their collapsing position. This view sees fascism as a sinister special tool used by financial and industrial imperialists.

Between these two extreme interpretations of the social foundations of fascism, there is no compromise or sound explanation. Liberals and democrats also fail to see the means and the ends; they begin with preconceived notions about the terror and dictatorship spread by fascism, and the resulting analysis has nothing to do with the implicit political cooperation that is involved. Because this is not a theological issue, nor a matter of logic, but a movement issue, a socio-economic issue, that guides civilized people to exercise or accept certain political behaviors.

The fascists themselves do not provide much clarification on this issue. As they themselves say, they are focused on creating history rather than writing it. The British fascist—and also a shrewd historian—Arendt addresses Strachey's argument with a dismissive tone. At the same time, he himself proposes an interpretation of fascism. In the writings most sympathetic to fascism, his words can be described as one of the most typical. He said: "In the current critical moment when the speed of the crisis is awakening the people, fascism is appealing equally to two kinds of people, one is the middle class, who is temperamentally conservative and spiritually has a strong national idea of the will of the young, and the other is a more innovative view, and will be disappointed and angered by the left-wing leaders who can not achieve their wishes of the fewer, more active individuals."

Although these words are very vague, they reveal many questions that must be answered before one can guess the viability of fascism and whether it is suitable for other countries. Is the passion behind the fascist movement entirely composed of amplifiers and salute exercises? Can the abandoned middle class finally organize itself and gain power? Although the middle class has not played the role of the ruling class in Western European society for more than a hundred years, has it spread its ideals and its values so widely that monopolists still dream of becoming small capitalists?

The final answer to these questions should be given by fascism itself. It depends on how it chooses between the small citizens who vote for it and the bankers and industrialists who support it, or how it succeeds in avoiding a choice.

Countries that have not yet tested fascism can get a relatively quick answer. This answer must be based on a more thorough study and analysis of the middle class than is currently common. This analysis, first, will rewrite the history of the middle class, especially in relation to the capitalist class and the proletariat. Second, it will expose the roots of the economic power of the middle class, and will understand how the vitality of the middle class is expanding through commercial or geographical boundaries. Without such an analysis, even the terminology of fascism cannot be used as a reliable tool for making people aware.

Songjiang

Director Yu of the Department Inspects Police Officers

The spring inspection of public security police officers in the nine counties of Songjiang District was originally commissioned to Administrative Inspector Commissioner Wang Gongyu as the representative inspector, with personnel assigned to assist. Now, the commissioner has received a telegram from Director Yu of the Department, informing him that he will personally come to Songjiang on the 10th to conduct the inspection. All accompanying personnel will arrive in Songjiang on the 9th and stay at the Xin Songjiang Society dormitory.

District One Prepares to Dredge the City River

The city river in this county was dredged last year under the auspices of the Chenghuang Dredging River Committee. However, due to various complications, three sections were left uncompleted. After Magistrate Li took office, he immediately transferred the Dredging Committee to the First District Office, ordering them to prepare for the work. He also dispatched the chief of the Third Section to survey the main and tributary river channels, draw up charts, and issue orders for implementation. The First District Office has now invited bids for dredging. The river channel from Fenghuangshan Bridge outside the West Gate to Bailongtan River is estimated to be 3123.75 cubic meters of earth, the bottom of Hulong Bridge and the Hetai Weir River is estimated to be 569.25 cubic meters of earth, the power company to the West Suspension Bridge is estimated to be 1698 cubic meters of earth, the West Suspension Bridge to Fenghuangshan Bridge River is estimated to be 2805 cubic meters of earth, and the West Shuiguan Bridge to Tao Xing Bridge is estimated to be 7486.9 cubic meters of earth. The bidding for the dam construction and water lifting project will be opened publicly on the afternoon of the 20th.

Lascivious Monk Dies of Illness in Mistress's Home

Hengpei, the abbot of Chao Guo Temple, was over thirty years old and fond of women. He had two mistresses in Songjiang. Yesterday, the monk died of illness at the home of his mistress, A Bao, at No. 4 Huashuhang Alley, Mo Family Lane. The news spread far and wide, causing astonishment. Later, the monks from the temple carried the body back to the temple for encoffining.

Kunshan

Boat Capsizing Tragedy Occurs at Jian Shan Lake

Dianshan Lake, located near Jinjiazhuang in the Fifth District of the county, spans over six li. Due to continuous strong winds, a boat capsizing tragedy occurred around 7 PM on the 8th. Over thirty boats sank, mostly stone boats. Countless people drowned.

Suzhou

Lawyer He Qi Released on Bail in Suzhou

Since assuming office, Zhu Shusheng, the president of the Jiangsu High Court, has had an excellent reputation. However, in February of this year, he was attacked by Zhu Xiongwu, a former clerk of the Jiangsu High Court who had been dismissed from his position, and others, in the name of the Jiangsu Judicial Improvement Association, who printed and distributed a large number of pamphlets. After investigation, it was discovered that Zhu Xiongwu and others were responsible. The High Procuratorate dispatched a prosecutor to search Zhu Xiongwu's residence and discovered evidence of bribery and malpractice during Zhu Xiongwu's tenure. Zhu Xiongwu was handed over to the Wuxian District Court Procuratorate for investigation. After the investigation by Prosecutor Lü, Chen Chaozan, a former clerk of the Qingjiangpu First Branch Court, and lawyer Lu Wenguang were also arrested and detained on suspicion. Chen Shitao, a criminal court judge of the Wuxi County Court, was also suspected of accepting bribes and was ordered to be released on bail. Various related parties were summoned for interrogation multiple times. On the afternoon of the 8th, Ji Yunqing and others from Wuxi were summoned for investigation, asked about everything, and then ordered to return. It was then learned that lawyer He Qi, residing at No. 98 Garden Lane, Jin Shenfu Road, Shanghai, was also a major suspect. A secret telegram was sent to the Shanghai Second Special District Court to arrest He Qi. On the night of the 8th, He Qi was escorted from Shanghai to Suzhou. Upon arrival at the District Court, because it was too late, no one was responsible, so he temporarily stayed at the Jingde Road Garden Hotel that night. On the morning of the 9th, he was escorted to the District Court, where Prosecutor Lü opened court for investigation, ordering him to be released on bail after providing a guarantor. It is said that the reason for He Qi's arrest was that the correspondence between He Qi and Chen Chaozan seemed to be related. He had been summoned twice, but He refused to appear, so he was arrested.

Notorious Bandit Li Genbao Arrested. Li Genbao, a notorious bandit from Taihu, a native of Shuzhuang, committed numerous crimes in the lakeside villages. In November of last year, the thirteen major robbery cases in Manshan, Taihu, were also committed by this bandit and his gang. The search and arrest were unsuccessful. Zhou, the district chief of the Second District of the Water Public Security Bureau, had consulted with the Wujiang and Wuxi counties and instructed the water police under his jurisdiction to strictly apprehend the bandit. Shao, the captain of the investigation team of the Wujiang Branch Public Security Bureau, learned that the bandit was hiding in Dongshan, Dongting. He immediately dispatched detectives and successfully captured the bandit, escorting him to the team headquarters. According to the interrogation, he confessed to robbing Zhou Pinzhang's family in Dongshan, obtaining over a thousand yuan to share, and admitted to robbing Manshan and other places. He was sent to the Wujiang County Government on the 9th and will be sent to the Second District of the Water Public Security Bureau within days for interrogation.

Police and Bandits Engage in Fierce Battle in Heavy Storm

Ding Changbao of Chenmu, Suzhou, was kidnapped by bandits some time ago. Later, a letter came demanding a large ransom. Ding's family reported it to the local police station. A patrol officer led the police, disguised as civilians, to patrol the area by boat. In a heavy storm on the night of the 8th, they engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits in the Wusong River for two hours. One bandit was captured, two bandits were shot, and two bandits were killed.

Wuxi

Lake Bandits Discovered in Wutang Township

Wutang Township in the Third District of the county is located near Taihu Lake and is strategically important, often frequented by lake bandits. The day before yesterday evening, more than thirty hooded boats suddenly arrived, fully loaded with seventy or eighty lake bandits, equipped with complete firearms and weapons such as machine guns and steel cannons. They intended to enter the port and rob. The incident was discovered by Lu Difan, the director of the local lookout post, who immediately notified all the post members to arm themselves for defense and notified the Nanfangquan lookout post to be on strict alert. He also came to the city overnight to report to the county for instructions. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Long dispatched more than two hundred soldiers from the security brigade yesterday to pursue and suppress the bandits. However, the lake bandits had already fled far away. The team returned to the county to report back.

Chu Minyi Visits Changzhou for Sightseeing

Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, along with Zhang Qidong, the general director of the Shanghai Chinese Sports Association, Xu Hui, a sports figure, and others, arrived in Changzhou from Nanjing on the evening of the 7th. On the morning of the 8th, Sun Youguang, the director of the Education Bureau, accompanied them to visit Qingliang Temple in the southern suburbs and Tianning Temple, Hongmei Pavilion, and Zhaozhou Pavilion in the eastern suburbs. In the afternoon at two o'clock, Chu went to visit the Industrial and Learning Group and Zhengde Vocational School in the Second Park of Wen Zai Men. Cheng Lie and Wu and others held a meeting to welcome him. Chu wrote and presented the Industrial and Learning Group with the eight characters "Labor, Service, Revival, Nation." He also discussed Taijiquan and other skills with the Zhengde Vocational School. Around four o'clock, Director Sun gathered teachers and students from various schools in the urban area at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall and invited Chu to give a speech on "The Purpose and Methods of Sports." After the speech, he performed Taijiquan, followed by a performance of Taiji exercises. At eight o'clock in the evening, he left Changzhou by car for Wuxi.

Qingpu

Corrections to the Land Survey Notice

Citizens Ye Lifeng and Zhu Sishi of Liantang, Daxiao Zheng, and others in the Third District of Qingpu submitted a petition to Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating: The Qingpu County Land Bureau has made numerous errors in handling the land survey, making registration impossible. For example, the notice only has the new number and no old number, making it impossible for people to verify, mistake one. Also, the boundaries of the land are not filled in, or if they are, they do not match the fish-scale register, mistake two. Also, the land in Figure 58 of District 3, Ward 41, was mistakenly entered into Figures 53 and 54, causing confusion and making it impossible to investigate, mistake three. Also, some notices write Fengjing Xu, and some write Liantang Xu, but Fengjing and Liantang are both town names and not Xu names. Such carelessness makes it difficult for people to register. We are now planning remedial measures and request that the County Bureau correct the notices, based on the fish-scale register and the Qingpu County Continued Records, which contain the boundaries of the Figures and Xu and the old numbers, and send them again to facilitate registration.

Nantong

Implement Zonal Coastal Fishery Protection

The yellow croaker season is approaching on the Jiangbei coast. The provincial government, to prevent sea bandits from disturbing the area, ordered the major detachments of the Third District of the Provincial Water Public Security Bureau to go to sea to protect fishing. District Chief Zhu Aizhou has specifically divided the fishing area according to the fishing season and assigned each detachment to be responsible. Chief Inspector Shen is the commander-in-chief of the fishery protection team, and police ships such as the Jun He and Ce Dian assist in patrolling.

Utilize Baojia to Popularize Literacy

Nantong's urban and rural areas are currently using the Baojia system to promote universal literacy. All illiterate men and women are divided into classes and forced to attend school. Special literacy classes have also been organized for prostitutes in the Southeast Camp area, with two hours of lessons per day and graduation in four months. If prostitutes fail to attend without a valid reason, the Public Security Bureau will dispatch police to summon them.

Change of Special Commissioner's Military Judge

The Nantong District Administrative Inspector Commissioner's Office has established a military court to try and sentence those convicted of opium, drugs, and banditry. Military Judge Zhu Feiru has firmly resigned. Special Commissioner Ge Tan submitted a report to the Provincial Government for approval. It has now been approved, and Chu Kaihu, a native of Yixing, has been appointed to replace him. Chu arrived in Tong on the 6th to take up his duties.

Pinghu

Hail and Continuous Rain Cause Disaster

On the morning of the 7th in this county, the weather was extremely hot. At 5 PM, there was a sudden rainstorm, and hailstones as large as a dog's head suddenly fell from the sky, lasting for about ten minutes. Eight or nine out of ten rural cart sheds were destroyed, and the spring crops were completely ruined. Many pedestrians were injured in the head. The glass skylights in the city were all destroyed, and women and children were crying in unison. On the morning of the 8th, the weather was hot again. At 1 PM, a sudden heavy rain came, accompanied by strong winds. Within an hour, the temperature dropped by more than twenty degrees, and the streets were full of puddles. Pedestrians were wading through the water with their clothes lifted. According to elderly people in their sixties and seventies, they have never seen such a disaster in their lives.

Local News

Garrison Command Orders Proclamation Urging Smokers to Register Universally. This is a Special Measure During the Reporting Period

The Songhu Garrison Command recently received a telegram from the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission and Chief Prohibition Commissioner, Chiang, on the prohibition methods of February 25, stating: The purpose of organizing smoker registration was to obtain accurate statistics in order to determine the standards for phased prohibition. However, since the end of registration at the end of last year, many cases of private opium smoking have occurred in various places, proving that the smoker registration conducted in various provinces, cities, and counties still has omissions. Therefore, the Measures for Reporting Smoker Registration have been specially formulated, and in February, the general principles of reporting and the strict enforcement of registration were ordered. Now, to implement the meaning of reporting and promote universal registration, it is specifically stipulated that provincial, city, and county governments, garrison security commands, and other military agencies authorized to conduct military trials, for cases of private opium smoking discovered since January 1 of this year, that have already been sentenced, regardless of whether they have been executed or not, or that have not yet been approved, should uniformly revoke the original judgment. All cases that have been discovered but not yet sentenced should be ordered to register in accordance with Article 3 of the Measures for Reporting Smoker Registration, exempt from punishment, and released immediately after registering and receiving a license to avoid unnecessary burdens. This is a special measure during the reporting period. After the reporting is completed, the procedures for handling cases of private opium smoking will be ordered separately. In addition to sending a telegram, the Geng telegram and reporting measures are attached for immediate compliance and to be forwarded to subordinates for strict compliance. After receiving the order, Commander Yang, in addition to complying, promulgated it on the 8th for general knowledge.

Garrison Command Releases a Large Number of Opium Offenders

A Last Opportunity for Self-Renewal. Ordered to Re-Register, Temporarily Provide a Guarantee and Release. The Public Security Bureau Discusses General Reporting Steps Yesterday Morning. Dagong Society Reports: The Songhu Garrison Command, to give opium smokers a last opportunity for self-renewal, specially obtained approval from the Military Affairs Commission to release over 300 opium offenders in detention with lighter circumstances on bail, returning them to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for re-licensing. The city's general reporting of opium smokers was discussed yesterday morning to proceed. Details are as follows:

Overcrowding in Detention Centers

The city's opium prohibition work, since its beginning on July 1 of last year, has been carried out diligently by the Municipal Public Security Bureau in accordance with the Military Affairs Commission's opium prohibition measures, divided into voluntary and compulsory periods. Over 30,000 people have registered. Since the registration deadline, strict investigation work has been carried out, breaking over 300 opium dens and arresting over 800 opium offenders. All have been interrogated by the Municipal Public Security Bureau and sent to the Songhu Garrison Command for judgment and detention. However, the Garrison Command, due to limited detention center space, has caused overcrowding of opium offenders, resulting in difficulties in detention. The details have been reported to the Military Affairs Commission for review and handling.

Opium Offenders Renew Themselves

The command recently received an order from the Military Affairs Commission regarding the release of detained opium offenders who have been sentenced or not, returning them to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for re-licensing and registration, temporarily providing a guarantee and releasing them. The command has now released over 300 male and female opium offenders with lighter circumstances, returning them to the Public Security Bureau to handle the re-licensing procedures. Those with more serious crimes will be transferred to detoxification centers for detoxification, then released with a guarantee. This is giving opium offenders a last opportunity for self-renewal. If they are arrested a second time or reported by someone and the results of the investigation show that they are still smoking opium, they will be punished by military law.

Discussion of Reporting

Since the Regulations for Reporting Opium Smokers were issued by the Opium Prohibition Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission, the Opium Prohibition Department of the Municipal Public Security Bureau convened a meeting of all personnel at 10 AM yesterday to study each article of the reporting regulations and formulate implementation steps. The general reporting period will begin within days.

Random Checks at Any Time

In recent days, the city's military and police authorities have intensified their work on the opium prohibition movement. The methods for reporting opium smoking by personnel of various agencies, public officials, and staff of mass organizations are also detailed in the reporting regulations. The first step is to request various agencies and organizations to report voluntarily, and then give them a considerable amount of time to quit smoking. Then, random checks will be conducted at any time. If they are found to be smoking again, they will be dismissed and punished.

Large-Scale Anti-Smoking Campaign

Municipal Party Department Passes Preparatory Measures, Propaganda Week to Be Held Starting on the 20th, With Separate Parades and Lantern Parades, First Preparatory Meeting Scheduled for the 14th

The implementation of rejecting drugs and prohibiting smoking is being actively carried out in various regions, with remarkable results. This city has also been proceeding step by step under the Public Security Bureau, and registration procedures have long been completed. Currently, investigations are underway. The Municipal Party Department of this city believes that rejecting drugs and prohibiting smoking requires the united effort of all, to eradicate the roots. Most smokers are ignorant and uninformed, and given the mix of Chinese and foreigners in this city, it easily affects other areas. It is imperative to conduct a major publicity campaign, hoping that all citizens will have a considerable understanding of the authorities' anti-smoking efforts, so as to eliminate the poisonous atmosphere within the scheduled time limit. Therefore, in accordance with the central government's instructions, the department has drafted publicity measures, intending to unite with all sectors to conduct a large-scale propaganda week, lantern parades, and extraordinary publicity. It is now heard that the measures, etc., were approved by the Executive Committee yesterday, and the first preparatory meeting is scheduled for the afternoon of the 14th. Details are as follows:

Organizational Regulations

"Organizational Regulations of the Shanghai Anti-Smoking and Drug Rejection Propaganda Preparatory Committee," Article 1: This committee is designated as the Shanghai Anti-Smoking and Drug Rejection Propaganda Preparatory Committee. Article 2: This committee upholds the central government's intentions and aims to expand anti-smoking and drug rejection propaganda in this city. Article 3: This committee is organized by ten institutions and legal entities, including the Municipal Party Department, Municipal Government, Public Security Bureau, Command Headquarters, Shanghai Anti-Smoking Committee, Municipal Farmers' Association, General Labor Union, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Municipal Education Association, and National Drug Rejection Association. Article 4: This committee shall have ten executive officers, to be held by the initiating institutions and legal entities. Article 5: The executive officers shall elect three standing executive officers to preside over daily affairs. Article 6: The standing executive officers shall establish four sections: document, finance, design, and propaganda. Article 7: The scope of work of each section of this committee is as follows: Document: Under the guidance of the standing executive officers, handle the committee's document matters. Finance: Manage the committee's financial revenue and expenditure matters. Design: Handle various propaganda design matters. Propaganda: Responsible for various matters related to propaganda. Article 8: The detailed rules for each section of this committee shall be formulated by each section and implemented after approval by the standing executive officers. Article 9: The work plan of this committee shall be formulated separately. Article 10: The initial budget of this committee is tentatively set at seven hundred yuan, to be apportioned by the Municipal Government, Public Security Bureau, Command Headquarters, Anti-Smoking Committee, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Municipal Party Department. Article 11: The address of this committee is temporarily set at the Municipal Party Department. Article 12: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they shall be proposed by the executive officers and revised by the executive officers' meeting. Article 13: These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the executive officers' meeting.

Implementation Plan

"Implementation Plan for the Work of the Shanghai Anti-Smoking and Drug Rejection Propaganda Preparatory Committee," (1) This plan is formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the committee's organizational regulations. (2) This plan takes the propaganda guidelines indicated in the Central Propaganda Department's Special Character No. 5 Propaganda Communication as the scope of work. (3) This committee designates April 20th to April 26th as the Anti-Smoking and Drug Rejection Propaganda Week in this city, with the following schedule: Day 1 (April 20th): All-Sector Propaganda Day, enlarged commemorative week in the morning, parade in the afternoon (route to be determined separately). Day 2 (April 21st): Party Department Propaganda Day, (A) the Municipal Party Department orders subordinate party departments to organize propaganda teams to set out for propaganda, (B) the Party Department broadcasts speeches. Day 3 (April 22nd): Academic Sector Propaganda Day, (A) the Municipal Education Association guides students from various schools to organize propaganda teams to set out for propaganda, (B) celebrities broadcast speeches. Day 4 (April 23rd): Storytelling and Broadcast Propaganda Day, (A) borrow teahouse gathering places, (B) humorous broadcast propaganda. Day 5 (April 24th): Film Propaganda Day, (A) public places screen anti-drug films, (B) theaters screen anti-smoking and drug rejection propaganda slides. Day 6 (April 25th): Entertainment Propaganda Day, jointly organized by the Municipal Farmers' Association, General Labor Union, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, National Drug Rejection Association, and Municipal Anti-Smoking Committee. Day 7 (April 26th): Lantern Propaganda Day, in the name of the preparatory committee, send letters to various institutions, organizations, schools, and party departments in this city to participate, detailed measures to be determined separately. (4) Send letters to major and minor newspapers in this city, requiring them to write editorials on anti-smoking and drug rejection propaganda on April 20th, and to write more articles and drawings on the said propaganda during the propaganda week. (5) Send a letter to the Municipal Education Bureau, ordering the directors of student affairs in various schools in this city to designate the anti-smoking and drug rejection propaganda as one of the students' holiday assignments, with the method taking each student's family as the center, and then extensively penetrating the public, so that they deeply recognize the government's determination to prohibit smoking and drugs, and use the Interim Regulations on Punishment for Smoking as propaganda material, so that they know that planting, transporting, selling, and smoking are illegal acts that should not be tried. (6) Prepare a letter and send personnel to contact the Aviation Association, requesting them to send several airplanes to distribute colorful slogans during the parade on the afternoon of the All-Sector Propaganda Day. (7) The regulations for various propaganda materials are as follows: (1) Slogans: to be posted on major traffic routes, (2) Pictures: same as above, (3) Propaganda pamphlets: to be distributed during parades and gatherings, (4) Colorful slogans: to be distributed by airplanes, (5) Other. (8) When gathering for parades, each group must bring its own slogans and flags. During the lantern parade, lamps, candles, and other items shall also be self-provided. (9) If there are any matters not covered in this plan, they shall be revised by the executive officers' meeting at any time. (10) This plan shall be implemented after being approved by the preparatory committee's executive officers' meeting.

First Preparatory Meeting

After the Municipal Party Department submitted the above regulations and plan to the Executive Committee for approval yesterday, in order to actively proceed and allow for ample preparation, it has been decided to convene representatives from relevant institutions and organizations at 2:00 PM on the 14th of this month (Tuesday) in the conference room of the department to determine positions, allocate work, and actively carry out preparations, it is said.
